                      <div data-reactid="507">
                       Private upstairs room and new bath, queen bed (or twin bedroom available just specify), in historic home near campus, restaurants &amp; coffee shop nearby. Sitting area adjoining room. Complimentary, coffee,tea &amp; snacks in room. Purified whole house water. Convenient location to college and town square. Second bedroom available across landing with twin beds for primary guest's use only. If you need two rooms just book a third person (It will be a little less $ for the second room).
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="508">
                       Our guest room looks south toward the college campus, we are fairly high up and you can see the town steeples and courthouse dome in the winter (east) hence our name "Steeplechase" and the fact that we are timber racing fans. The room has hardwood floors and very tall windows with antique glass. The bed is a queen size with a brand new pillow top mattress. The new bath is off of the sitting area/landing just outside the door to the room. It has a shower, toilet and pedestal sink. We have a whole house RainSoft water filter system. (extra Twin Beds room now also available see Summary) Ask for a special deal for longer term stays. I always book through AirBnB.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="509">
                       Adjacent to Martin Methodist College and other historic homes and close proximity to downtown Pulaski. There are wonderful simple cafe type restaurants to walk to, The Yellow Deli, Savory Jack's, Buckhead Coffee, The Bluebird Cafe, SILK. Star Theatre (plays) and The Martin (movies) are within three blocks. Cathy's Tavern is a famous nightspot for country music nearby.

                     <div data-reactid="811">
                      <div data-reactid="812">
                       The Cozy Lavender Cottage is located on a farm. 1860s Charm. A few miles down the road from the famous Jack Daniel's Distillery, and antique shopper's paradise Fayetteville, TN. Music City Nashville is a scenic drive of about an hour, and 30 miles from Huntsville, and its aerospace. The area is known for its Antebellum, Georgian, and Victorian houses, Antique Shopping, as well as the Tennessee Walking Horse and Tennessee Mules.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="813">
                       The farm at one time was owned by Civil War Hero (and brother of Jack) Wiley Daniel and his heirs. Mulberry Creek runs right by the farm and is a fun place to watch the water and have a picnic. The farm has a very park-like setting with pastoral views, wooded areas and walking trails. The farm grows lavender, vegetables, and hay. There are Navajo Churro Sheep doing the weeding, and an assortment of heirloom poultry and geese.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="814">
                       The farm is in a quiet area but with easy access to Hwy 50/55, I-64, and I-65. The nearest towns where you can shop, get groceries, and dine are Fayetteville, and Lynchburg. A fun place for a good cup of coffee and something other than BBQ is Southern Perks on the square of Lynchburg. In these smaller towns, the stores often close early so try to get there in the morning.

                      <div data-reactid="1382">
                       A beautiful two-story 100 y ear old farmhouse, recently restored and one mile off the square in downtown historic Fayetteville, Tn. A short drive to Lynchburg and Jack Daniels distillery and Tims Ford dam. three bedrooms, three kitchens and 3300 sq
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1383">
                       This 3300 square ft. historic 100 yr old farmhouse has a 9 foot spacious wrap-around porch for good quality relaxing and rocking. Three bedrooms that will sleep 9 and we have antique furnishings throughout. With three kitchens and plenty of tables in the dining room renters can have a perfect space for hosting their own events, like bridal showers or corporate events. There are eight fireplaces and 2 and half baths, one with an antique claw ft. tub for soaking and fitted with shower. There are lots of beautiful details with murals painted throughout,vintage wall paper,oak pocket doors, hand cut wood floors, leaded window and chandeliers throughout for an elegant step back in history. The couple that owns the home has a section of the house that has become their own apartment, but in certain circumstances this can also be rented.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1384">
                       This house is right in the middle of historic homes ,but close enough to main square of Fayettville to feel like part of the town . Pastures on the front corners of the house make it feel like you are still in the country.
